    //Method used in acc.product.js
    function addToCartPage(itemId, sku) {
        let R3_COMMON = getCommon();
        R3_COMMON.addPlacementType('add_to_cart_page');
        R3_COMMON.setPageBrand('ESIKA');

        

        var R3_ADDTOCART = new r3_addtocart();
        R3_ADDTOCART.addItemIdToCart(sku);

        rr_flush_onload();
        r3();
        resetR3();
    }
    //Method used in acc.product.js

    function resetR3() {
        if (typeof window.R3_COMMON !== 'undefined') { window.R3_COMMON = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_ITEM !== 'undefined') { window.R3_ITEM = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_PURCHASED !== 'undefined') { window.R3_PURCHASED = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_HOME !== 'undefined') { window.R3_HOME = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_SEARCH !== 'undefined') { window.R3_SEARCH = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_CATEGORY !== 'undefined') { window.R3_CATEGORY = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_BRAND !== 'undefined') { window.R3_BRAND = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_ADDTOCART !== 'undefined') { window.R3_ADDTOCART = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_CART !== 'undefined') { window.R3_CART = undefined; }
        if (typeof window.R3_GENERIC !== 'undefined') { window.R3_GENERIC = undefined; }
    }

    function loadCarrouselForDefault(){
        let R3_COMMON = getCommon();
        R3_COMMON.addPlacementType("search_page.live_box");
        R3_COMMON.setPageBrand('ESIKA');

        var R3_SEARCH = new r3_search();
    }

    function getUrlParameterByName(name, url = window.location.href) {
        name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\$&');
        var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
            results = regex.exec(url);
        if (!results) return null;
        if (!results[2]) return '';
        return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
    }

<div class="panel-heading">
<div class="panel-title">
<div class="panel-title__head active" data-toggle="collapse" href="#collapse0">
<h2 bucket-positon="Bloque 1">Descripción</h2>
<div class="panel-title__plus"></div>
<div class="panel-title__minus"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="collapse0" class="panel-collapse collapse in"> <div class="panel-body">
<p class="panel-body__description"> Perfume masculino diseñado con exclusivas notas de cuero italiano y aromáticas notas de ciprés. Para el hombre exitoso y sofisticado; él sabe que el éxito radica en saber elegir. Aroma maderoso, de muy alta concentración y larga duración. Capacidad 90 ml</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel">
<div class="panel-heading">
<div class="panel-title">
<div class="panel-title__head" data-toggle="collapse" href="#collapse1">
<h2 bucket-positon="Bloque 2">Notas Olfativas</h2>
<div class="panel-title__plus"></div>
<div class="panel-title__minus"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="collapse1" class="panel-collapse collapse">
<div class="panel-body">
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Notas de Salida: Hojas de violeta, manzana crujiente, cardamomo negro y salvia.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Notas de Cuerpo: Lirio de agua, geranio, cedro, flor de naranja y whisky.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Notas de Fondo: Sándalo, madera de guaiac, musk, cuero italiano, ámbar gris y musgo</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Ingredientes: Cuero italiano y ciprés.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> ¿Cuál es el secreto de la calidad y duración de nuestras fragancias? Essent Tech*. El proceso de fabricación de fragancias en el que se define el tiempo ideal de maceración, la parte más crítica al hacer una fragancia, para maximizar su aroma y duración. Trabajamos con estrictos controles de calidad, con lo último en tecnología y con los mejores perfumistas del mundo, que garantizan la calidad de nuestros aromas. * “Proceso de fabricación de fragancias no incluye: kit de nuevas, expofertas y productos de línea con campaña de descontinuación establecida”.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel">
<div class="panel-heading">
<div class="panel-title">
<div class="panel-title__head" data-toggle="collapse" href="#collapse2">
<h2 bucket-positon="Bloque 3">Concepto</h2>
<div class="panel-title__plus"></div>
<div class="panel-title__minus"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="collapse2" class="panel-collapse collapse">
<div class="panel-body">
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Cada detalle refleja su buen gusto. Él sabe que el lujo y el aroma del éxito se disfrutan lentamente. Le gusta lo mejor de lo mejor.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Aplicación: Aplica el perfume después de salir de la ducha para una mejor penetración del aroma.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Para mayor duración del aroma, aplica crema hidrante previamente. De preferencia, que sea del mismo aroma del perfume.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Para una mejor conservación, guárdalo en un lugar ventilado donde no reciba luz directa.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="panel">
<div class="panel-heading">
<div class="panel-title">
<div class="panel-title__head" data-toggle="collapse" href="#collapse3">
<h2 bucket-positon="Bloque 4">¿Dónde aplicar el perfume?</h2>
<div class="panel-title__plus"></div>
<div class="panel-title__minus"></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="collapse3" class="panel-collapse collapse">
<div class="panel-body">
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Úsalo en ocasiones especiales. Intensifica el aroma, aplicando el perfume detrás de las orejas, en las muñecas y la clavícula.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Para una mejor conservación, guárda el perfume en un lugar ventilado, donde no reciba luz directa.</p>
<p class="panel-body__descriptionBucket"> Notas de Fondo: Sándalo, madera de guaiac, musk, cuero italiano, ámbar gris y musgo</p>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">

        function getCarrouselitem_page_esika1(orderCarousel) {
            repaintCarrouselitem_page_esika1(richRelevencePlacements['item_page.esika1'], 'item_page_esika1-carrousel', orderCarousel);
        }

        function repaintCarrouselitem_page_esika1(placements, idCarrousel, orderCarousel) {
            if (placements != null && placements != "") {

                var carousel = document.querySelector(".carrouselRichRelevance-item_page_esika1");

                var containerTemplate = getContainerTemplateitem_page_esika1(placements, idCarrousel);

                carousel.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', containerTemplate);


                var listProduct = document.querySelector("." + idCarrousel);
                var strategy = placements.strategy;
                var message = placements.message;

                var position = 1;
                placements.items.forEach(product => {
                    var newproduct = getProductTemplateitem_page_esika1(product, strategy, message, orderCarousel, position);
                    listProduct.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', newproduct);
                    position++;
                });
            }
        }

        function getRatingTemplateitem_page_esika1(active) {
            return `<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-star ${active}"></span>`;
        }

        function getContainerTemplateitem_page_esika1(firstCarrousel, idClass) {
            return ` <h3 class="headline"> ${firstCarrousel.message}</h3>
                <div class="carousel-component carousel-crosseling rich-relevance">
                    <div class="carousel js-owl-carousel-RichRelevance js-owl-carousel ${idClass}"></div>
                </div>`;
        }

        function getProductTemplateitem_page_esika1(product, strategy, message, orderCarousel, position) {
            var formatPriceitem_page_esika1;
            var formatSalePriceitem_page_esika1;
            if (product.salePrice == product.price) {
                formatSalePriceitem_page_esika1 = tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.salePrice);
                formatPriceitem_page_esika1 = "";
            } else {
                formatSalePriceitem_page_esika1 = tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.salePrice);
                formatPriceitem_page_esika1 =  tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.price);
            }
            return `
                            <div class="item">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance" value="true">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_strategy" value="${strategy}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_message" value="${message}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_personalization" value="Personalización ${orderCarousel}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_id" value="${product.id}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_is_set" value="${product.isSet}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_is_variable_set" value="${product.isVariableSet}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_position" value="${position}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_strategy" value="${product.strategyCode}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_category" value="${product.mainCategory}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_cuv" value="${product.cuv}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_currencyIso" value="${product.currencyISO}">
                                <a href="${product.linkURL}" title="${product.name}" >
                                    <div class="thumb">
                                         <img class="lazyOwl item" data-src="${product.imageURL}" alt="${product.name}" title="${product.name}"/>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="item-name">${product.name}</div>
                                    <div class="priceContainer">
                                        <span>${formatPriceitem_page_esika1}</span>
                                        <span>${formatSalePriceitem_page_esika1}</span>
                                    </div>
                                </a>
                        </div>`;
        }


    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

        function getCarrouselitem_page_esika2(orderCarousel) {
            repaintCarrouselitem_page_esika2(richRelevencePlacements['item_page.esika2'], 'item_page_esika2-carrousel', orderCarousel);
        }

        function repaintCarrouselitem_page_esika2(placements, idCarrousel, orderCarousel) {
            if (placements != null && placements != "") {

                var carousel = document.querySelector(".carrouselRichRelevance-item_page_esika2");

                var containerTemplate = getContainerTemplateitem_page_esika2(placements, idCarrousel);

                carousel.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', containerTemplate);


                var listProduct = document.querySelector("." + idCarrousel);
                var strategy = placements.strategy;
                var message = placements.message;

                var position = 1;
                placements.items.forEach(product => {
                    var newproduct = getProductTemplateitem_page_esika2(product, strategy, message, orderCarousel, position);
                    listProduct.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', newproduct);
                    position++;
                });
            }
        }

        function getRatingTemplateitem_page_esika2(active) {
            return `<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-star ${active}"></span>`;
        }

        function getContainerTemplateitem_page_esika2(firstCarrousel, idClass) {
            return ` <h3 class="headline"> ${firstCarrousel.message}</h3>
                <div class="carousel-component carousel-crosseling rich-relevance">
                    <div class="carousel js-owl-carousel-RichRelevance js-owl-carousel ${idClass}"></div>
                </div>`;
        }

        function getProductTemplateitem_page_esika2(product, strategy, message, orderCarousel, position) {
            var formatPriceitem_page_esika2;
            var formatSalePriceitem_page_esika2;
            if (product.salePrice == product.price) {
                formatSalePriceitem_page_esika2 = tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.salePrice);
                formatPriceitem_page_esika2 = "";
            } else {
                formatSalePriceitem_page_esika2 = tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.salePrice);
                formatPriceitem_page_esika2 =  tagManagerObject.product.getPriceRichRelevance(product.price);
            }
            return `
                            <div class="item">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance" value="true">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_strategy" value="${strategy}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_message" value="${message}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_personalization" value="Personalización ${orderCarousel}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_id" value="${product.id}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_is_set" value="${product.isSet}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_is_variable_set" value="${product.isVariableSet}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_position" value="${position}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="product_rich_relevance_product_strategy" value="${product.strategyCode}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_category" value="${product.mainCategory}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_cuv" value="${product.cuv}">
                                <input type="hidden" name="productReference_currencyIso" value="${product.currencyISO}">
                                <a href="${product.linkURL}" title="${product.name}" >
                                    <div class="thumb">
                                         <img class="lazyOwl item" data-src="${product.imageURL}" alt="${product.name}" title="${product.name}"/>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="item-name">${product.name}</div>
                                    <div class="priceContainer">
                                        <span>${formatPriceitem_page_esika2}</span>
                                        <span>${formatSalePriceitem_page_esika2}</span>
                                    </div>
                                </a>
                        </div>`;
        }


    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	var analyticsConfig;
	if(typeof ACC != 'undefined'){
		analyticsConfig = ACC.addons.hybrisanalyticsaddon;
	}else{
		analyticsConfig = ACCMOB.addons.hybrisanalyticsaddon;
	}
	
	var piwikSiteId = "pe";
	var piwikTrackerUrl = "/pe\/events"; // Use Piwik HTTPS Endpoint by default
	var sessionId = "623bec41-fb10-4e43-8367-485bbfb274be";

	if(location.protocol != 'https:')	// if the current page does not use https protocol, use the normal HTTP endpoint:
	{
		piwikTrackerUrl = "/pe\/events";
	}

	var tracker = Piwik.getAsyncTracker(piwikTrackerUrl, piwikSiteId);

	tracker.setTrackerUrl(piwikTrackerUrl);
	tracker.setSiteId(piwikSiteId);
	tracker.setRequestMethod('POST');
	tracker.setRequestContentType('application/json; charset=UTF-8');

	var processPiwikRequest = (function (request) {
		try {
//console.log(request);
			var pairs = request.split('&');

			var requestParametersArray = {};
			for (index = 0; index < pairs.length; ++index) {
				var pair = pairs[index].split('=');
				requestParametersArray[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1] || '');
			}
			requestParametersArray['sessionId'] = sessionId;

			return JSON.stringify(requestParametersArray);
		} catch (err) {
			return request;
		}
	});

	tracker.setCustomRequestProcessing(processPiwikRequest);

	var hybrisAnalyticsPiwikPlugin = (function() {
		function _getEventtypeParam(suffix) { return '&eventtype=' + suffix; }
		function ecommerce() { return _getEventtypeParam("ecommerce"); }
		function event() { return _getEventtypeParam("event"); }
		function goal() { return _getEventtypeParam("goal"); }
		function link() { return _getEventtypeParam("link"); }
		function load() { return _getEventtypeParam("load"); }
		function log() { return _getEventtypeParam("log"); }
		function ping() { return _getEventtypeParam("ping"); }
		function run() { return _getEventtypeParam("run"); }
		function sitesearch() { return _getEventtypeParam("sitesearch"); }
		function unload() { return _getEventtypeParam("unload"); }

		return {
			ecommerce: ecommerce,
			event : event,
			goal : goal,
			link : link,
			load : load,
			log : log,
			ping: ping,
			sitesearch : sitesearch,
			unload : unload
		};
	})();
	tracker.addPlugin('hybrisAnalyticsPiwikPlugin', hybrisAnalyticsPiwikPlugin);
	// Hybris Analytics specifics - END


	
			//View Product event
			
				tracker.setEcommerceView('200100838',  // (required) SKU: Product unique identifier
								'Magnat',  // (optional) Product name
								['esika-020203','esika-020206'],  // (optional) Product category, or array of up to 5 categories
								'131.9');

				tracker.trackPageView('ViewProduct');  //Do we really need this ??
		

	tracker.enableLinkTracking();
	// handlers and their subscription for cart events


	function trackAddToCart_piwik(productCode, quantityAdded, cartData) {
		tracker.setEcommerceView(String(cartData.productCode),  // (required) SKU: Product unique identifier
				cartData.productName,  // (optional) Product name
				[ ], // (optional) Product category, string or array of up to 5 categories
				quantityAdded+""  // (optional, default to 1) Product quantity
		);
		tracker.addEcommerceItem(String(cartData.productCode),  // (required) SKU: Product unique identifier
				cartData.productName,  // (optional) Product name
				[ ], // (optional) Product category, string or array of up to 5 categories
				cartData.productPrice+"", // (recommended) Product price
				quantityAdded+""  // (optional, default to 1) Product quantity
		);

		if (!cartData.cartCode)
		{
			cartData.cartCode="";
		}
		tracker.setCustomVariable(1,"ec_id",cartData.cartCode,"page");
		tracker.trackEcommerceCartUpdate(
				'0'  // (required) Cart amount
		);
	}

	function trackBannerClick_piwik(url) {
		tracker.setCustomVariable(1,"bannerid",url,"page");
		tracker.trackLink(url, 'banner');
	}

	function trackContinueCheckoutClick_piwik() {
		tracker.setCustomVariable(1,"ec_id","","page");
		tracker.trackEvent('checkout', 'proceed', '','');
	}

    function trackShowReview_piwik() {
        tracker.trackEvent('review', 'view', '', '');
    }

	function trackUpdateCart_piwik(productCode,initialQuantity,newQuantity,cartData) {
		if (initialQuantity != newQuantity) {
			trackAddToCart_piwik(productCode, newQuantity,cartData);
		}
	}

	function trackRemoveFromCart_piwik(productCode, initialQuantity,cartData) {
		trackAddToCart_piwik(productCode, 0, cartData);
	}

	window.mediator.subscribe('trackAddToCart', function(data) {
		if (data.productCode && data.quantity) {
			trackAddToCart_piwik(data.productCode, data.quantity,data.cartData);
		}
	});

	window.mediator.subscribe('trackUpdateCart', function(data) {
		if (data.productCode && data.initialCartQuantity && data.newCartQuantity) {
			trackUpdateCart_piwik(data.productCode,data.initialCartQuantity,data.newCartQuantity,data);
		}
	});

	window.mediator.subscribe('trackRemoveFromCart', function(data) {
		if (data.productCode && data.initialCartQuantity) {
			trackRemoveFromCart_piwik(data.productCode, data.initialCartQuantity,data);
		}
	});

    window.mediator.subscribe('trackShowReviewClick', function() {
        trackShowReview_piwik();
    });

	$('.simple-banner').click(function(){
 		trackBannerClick_piwik( $(this).find("a").prop('href'));
	});

	$('.js-continue-checkout-button').click(function(){
		trackContinueCheckoutClick_piwik();
	});

</script>

          setAction('remove',data);

          setAction('update',data);

      function setAction(actionVar, data){
          var basket =
              {
  "quantity": 0,
  "total": {
    "value": 0,
    "currency": ""
  }
};

          

          var subtotalIncludingTaxVar =
              {
  "value": 0,
  "currency": ""
};

          var subtotalVar=
              {
  "value": 0,
  "currency": ""
};

          

          window.qproducts = [
              
          ]
          if(actionVar=='update'){
              window.qQuantity = data.newCartQuantity;
          }else{
              window.qQuantity = data.initialCartQuantity;
          }

          if(actionVar=='update' || actionVar=='remove'){
              var key = data.productCode;
              for (var key in window.qproducts) {
                  if (window.qproducts.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                      var actionjson = {
                          action:actionVar,
                          quantity:Number(window.qQuantity),
                          basket:basket,
                          subtotalIncludingTax:subtotalIncludingTaxVar,
                          subtotal:subtotalVar,
                          product:{
                              sku:window.qproducts[key].sku,
                              productId:window.qproducts[key].prdId,
                              name:window.qproducts[key].name,
                              manufacturer:window.qproducts[key].brand,
                              price:{
                                  value:Number(window.qproducts[key].price),
                                  currency:window.qproducts[key].currency
                              }
                          }};
                  }
              }

              
              uv.emit('ecBasketItemAction',actionjson);
              

          }

          if(actionVar=='add'){
              var totalQty = "";
              if(totalQty == '0'){
                  var subtotalIncludingTaxVar={
                      value:Number(data.cartData.productPrice),
                      currency:"PEN"
                  };

                  var subtotalVar={
                      value:Number(data.cartData.productPrice),
                      currency:"PEN"
                  };

                  var basket ={
                      quantity:1,
                      total:{
                          value:Number(data.cartData.productPrice),
                          currency:"PEN"
                      }
                  };

                  var basketAura ={
                      total:{
                          value:Number(data.cartData.productPrice),
                          currency:"PEN"
                      }
                  };
              }
              var actionjson = {
                  action:actionVar,
                  quantity:Number(data.quantity),
                  basket:basket,
                  subtotalIncludingTax: subtotalIncludingTaxVar,
                  subtotal:subtotalVar,
                  product:{
                      sku:data.cartData.productCode,
                      productId:data.cartData.productCode,
                      name:data.cartData.productName,
                      manufacturer:data.cartData.brand,
                      price:{
                          value:Number(data.cartData.productPrice),
                          currency:"PEN"
                      }
                  }
              };

              
              uv.emit('ecBasketItemAction',actionjson);
              
          }
      }


      </script>
